<FILENAME>d22806dex991.htm
<DESCRIPTION>EX-99.1
<TEXT>
<HTML><HEAD>
<TITLE>EX-99.1</TITLE>
</HEAD>
 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Apple Reports Record First Quarter Results </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>iPhone, Apple Watch,
Services&nbsp;&amp; Apple TV Drive All-time Record Revenue </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Results Produce Record Quarterly Profit of $18.4 Billion </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">CUPERTINO, California &#151; January&nbsp;26, 2016 &#151; Apple<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> today announced financial
results for its fiscal 2016 first quarter ended December&nbsp;26, 2015. The Company posted record quarterly revenue of $75.9 billion and record quarterly net income of $18.4 billion, or $3.28 per diluted share. These results compare to revenue of
$74.6 billion and net income of $18 billion, or $3.06 per diluted share, in the year-ago quarter. Gross margin was 40.1 percent compared to 39.9 percent in the year-ago quarter. International sales accounted for 66 percent of the quarter&#146;s
revenue. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">&#147;Our team delivered Apple&#146;s biggest quarter ever, thanks to the world&#146;s most innovative products and all-time record sales
of iPhone, Apple Watch and Apple TV,&#148; said Tim Cook, Apple&#146;s CEO. &#147;The growth of our Services business accelerated during the quarter to produce record results, and our installed base recently crossed a major milestone of one billion
active devices.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">&#147;Our record sales and strong margins drove all-time records for net income and EPS in spite of a very difficult
macroeconomic environment,&#148; said Luca Maestri, Apple&#146;s CFO. &#147;We generated operating cash flow of $27.5 billion during the quarter, and returned over $9 billion to investors through share repurchases and dividends. We have now
completed $153 billion of our $200 billion capital return program.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Apple is providing the following guidance for its fiscal 2016 second
quarter: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:9pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:9pt">revenue between $50 billion and $53 billion </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:9pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>

Company to deliver to the marketplace and stimulate customer demand for new programs, products, and technological innovations on a timely basis; the effect that product introductions and transitions, changes in product pricing or mix, and/or
increases in component costs could have on the Company&#146;s gross margin; the inventory risk associated with the Company&#146;s need to order or commit to order product components in advance of customer orders; the continued availability on
acceptable terms, or at all, of certain components and services essential to the Company&#146;s business currently obtained by the Company from sole or limited sources; the effect that the Company&#146;s dependency on manufacturing and logistics
services provided by third parties may have on the quality, quantity or cost of products manufactured or services rendered; risks associated with the Company&#146;s international operations; the Company&#146;s reliance on third-party intellectual
property and digital content; the potential impact of a finding that the Company has infringed on the intellectual property rights of others; the Company&#146;s dependency on the performance of distributors, carriers and other resellers of the
Company&#146;s products; the effect that product and service quality problems could have on the Company&#146;s sales and operating profits; the continued service and availability of key executives and employees; war, terrorism, public health issues,
natural disasters, and other circumstances that could disrupt supply, delivery, or demand of products; and unfavorable results of legal proceedings. More information on potential factors that could affect the Company&#146;s financial results is
included from time to time in the &#147;Risk Factors&#148; and &#147;Management&#146;s Discussion and Analysis of Financial Condition and Results of Operations&#148; sections of the Company&#146;s public reports filed with the SEC, including the
Company&#146;s Form 10-K for the fiscal year ended September&nbsp;26, 2015, and its Form 10-Q for the fiscal quarter ended December&nbsp;26, 2015 to be filed with the SEC. The Company assumes no obligation to update any forward-looking statements or
information, which speak as of their respective dates. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Apple revolutionized personal technology with the introduction of the Macintosh in 1984.
Today, Apple leads the world in innovation with iPhone, iPad, Mac, Apple Watch and Apple TV. Apple&#146;s four software platforms &#151; iOS, OS X, watchOS and tvOS &#151; provide seamless experiences across all Apple devices and empower people with
breakthrough services including the App Store, Apple Music, Apple Pay and iCloud. Apple&#146;s 100,000 employees are dedicated to making the best products on earth, and to leaving the world better than we found it. </P>

 </P> <P STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt"><FONT COLOR="#FFFFFF">Q1&#146;16 Earnings </FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Supplemental Material
</FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">January 26, 2016 </FONT></P>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt" ALIGN="center">


<IMG SRC="g22806ex99_3pg02.jpg" ALT="LOGO">

 </P> <P STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt"><FONT COLOR="#FFFFFF">Currency Index </FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">$100 of Apple&#146;s non-U.S.
dollar revenue in Q4&#146;14 translates into only $85 U.S. dollars today </FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Q4&#146;14 = 100 </FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">100 100
</FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">95 95 </FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">90 90 </FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">85 85
</FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Q4&#146;14 Q1&#146;16 </FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">The currency index is based on the average exchange rate per quarter
weighted by Apple&#146;s non-U.S. dollar revenue for each quarter. 1 </FONT></P>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt" ALIGN="center">


<IMG SRC="g22806ex99_3pg03.jpg" ALT="LOGO">

 </P> <P STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt"><FONT COLOR="#FFFFFF">Q1&#146;16 Constant Currency Revenue Growth
</FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">In constant currency, Q1&#146;16 revenue would have been $5 billion higher, reflecting an 8% Y/Y increase </FONT><br><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">$ in Billions </FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">As Reported In Constant Currency (1) </FONT><br><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Operating Segments Q1&#146;16 Revenue Q1&#146;15 Revenue (Non-GAAP) Y/Y Q1&#146;16 Revenue Y/Y (Non-GAAP) </FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Americas
$29.3 $30.6 -4% $30.2 -1% </FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Europe 17.9 17.2 4% 20.2 18% </FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Greater China 18.4 16.1 14% 19.0 17%
</FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Japan 4.8 5.4 -12% 5.3 -4% </FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Rest of Asia Pacific 5.4 5.2 4% 6.2 19% </FONT><br><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Total Apple $75.9 $74.6 2% $80.8 8% </FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Reconciliation from GAAP Revenue to Non-GAAP Constant Currency Revenue (1)
</FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Americas Europe Greater China Japan Rest of Asia Pacific Total Apple </FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Q1&#146;16 Revenue (GAAP)
$29.3 $17.9 $18.4 $4.8 $5.4 $75.9 </FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Foreign exchange effect on revenue 0.8 2.3 0.6 0.5 0.8 5.0
</FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Q1&#146;16 Constant Currency Revenue (Non-GAAP) $30.2 $20.2 $19.0 $5.3 $6.2 $80.8 </FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Q1&#146;15
Revenue (GAAP) $30.6 $17.2 $16.1 $5.4 $5.2 $74.6 </FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Constant Currency Revenue Growth (Non-GAAP) -1% 18% 17% -4% 19% 8% </FONT><br><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">(1) Apple calculates non-GAAP constant currency revenue by translating current quarter local currency revenue to U.S. dollars based on prior period average exchange rates. That amount is
compared to prior period GAAP revenue to derive non-GAAP constant currency revenue growth (expressed as a percentage). Apple considers non-GAAP constant currency revenue and revenue growth to be useful metrics to investors and management as they
facilitate a more useful comparison of current performance to historical performance. </FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Note: Numbers may not add precisely due to rounding. 2 </FONT></P>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt" ALIGN="center">


<IMG SRC="g22806ex99_3pg04.jpg" ALT="LOGO">

 </P> <P STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt"><FONT COLOR="#FFFFFF">Services Revenue </FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Apple&#146;s installed base
drove over $31 billion in related purchases in FY15, up 23% Y/Y, and almost $9 billion in Q1&#146;16, up 24% Y/Y </FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">$ in Billions FY14 FY15 Q1&#146;16 (1) </FONT><br><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Services Revenue $18.1 $19.9 $5.5 </FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Y/Y Change 10% 15% </FONT><br><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Services Revenue Driven by Installed Base: </FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">iTunes Purchased Content </FONT><br><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Apple Music </FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">App Store </FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Licensing
</FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Service PartsiCloud </FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Apple Pay </FONT><br><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Installed Base Related Revenue $14.9 $16.8 $4.7 </FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Adjustment to Reflect Certain Unrecognized Services Purchases (2)
$10.5 $14.3 $4.2 </FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Installed Base Related Purchases $25.3 $31.2 $8.9 </FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Y/Y Change 23% 24% </FONT><br><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">(1) Amounts exclude $548 million received from a patent infringement lawsuit. </FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">(2) For third-party applications
sold through the App Store and certain digital content sold through the iTunes Store, Apple accounts for such purchases on a net basis by recognizing in Services revenue only the commission it retains from each purchase. This non-GAAP adjustment
reflects the portion of the gross amounts billed to customers that Apple remits to third-party app developers and certain digital content owners. Apple considers non-GAAP installed base related purchases to be a useful metric for investors and
management as it provides a more complete picture of the transactions generated by the installed base. </FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Note: Numbers may not add precisely due to rounding. </FONT><br><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">3 </FONT></P>

<IMG SRC="g22806ex99_3pg05.jpg" ALT="LOGO">

 </P> <P STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt"><FONT COLOR="#FFFFFF">Active Installed Base </FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">1 Billion </FONT><br><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">iPhone, iPad, Mac, iPod touch, Apple TV, and Apple Watch devices </FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">that have been engaged with our services within
the past 90 days. </FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">4 </FONT></P>
